#

snmp-agent group v3 WangGuan privacy read-view WangGuan-RD notify-view WangGuan-NT
snmp-agent target-host host-name __targetHost_1_29621 trap address udp-domain 172.16.92.1 params securityname esight_admin v3 privacy
snmp-agent target-host host-name __targetHost_2_54678 trap address udp-domain 172.19.252.50 params securityname XT5@HzTeam&win v3 privacy
#

snmp-agent mib-view included WangGuan-RD internet
snmp-agent usm-user v3 esight_admin
snmp-agent usm-user v3 esight_admin group WangGuan
snmp-agent usm-user v3 esight_admin authentication-mode sha cipher %^%#o7|2Lj\skWGvhg(dNQU75/2;Lk9D9H;D$-1&@kb)%^%#
snmp-agent usm-user v3 esight_admin privacy-mode aes128 cipher %^%#hx{@N+dKqD:S-S%Z@WR(2ta<.`Z5j)oP1c8GddK~%^%#
snmp-agent usm-user v3 XT5@HzTeam&win

snmp-agent usm-user v3 XT5@HzTeam&win privacy-mode des56 cipher %^%#PA[^7YO.(U<%|@'oQ#v~hI25:a/x+L\L}$6;+A[H%^%#

# 配置SSH服务
stelnet ipv4 server enable
ssh user ww_admin
ssh user ww_admin authentication-type password
ssh user ww_admin service-type stelnet
ssh server-source all-interface
ssh ipv6 server-source all-interface
ssh server acl 2010
ssh authorization-type default aaa
#
ssh server cipher aes256_gcm aes128_gcm aes256_ctr aes192_ctr aes128_ctr
ssh server hmac sha2_512 sha2_256
ssh server key-exchange dh_group_exchange_sha256 dh_group_exchange_sha1 dh_group14_sha1 ecdh_sha2_nistp256 ecdh_sha2_nistp384 ecdh_sha2_nistp521
#
ssh server publickey ecc rsa
#
ssh server dh-exchange min-len 2048
#
ssh client publickey ecc rsa
#
ssh client cipher aes256_gcm aes128_gcm aes256_ctr aes192_ctr aes128_ctr
ssh client hmac sha2_512 sha2_256
ssh client key-exchange dh_group_exchange_sha256 dh_group_exchange_sha1 dh_group14_sha1 ecdh_sha2_nistp256 ecdh_sha2_nistp384 ecdh_sha2_nistp521

user-interface con 0

authentication-mode aaa
user privilege level 3
protocol inbound ssh
